**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/Strata--66225ca9`

- Use `github.com/sg-evals/Strata--66225ca9` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |

| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# big-code-strata-refac-001: Rename FxVanillaOption to FxEuropeanOption in OpenGamma Strata

## Task

Rename the `FxVanillaOption` type family to `FxEuropeanOption` throughout the OpenGamma Strata codebase. The `FxVanillaOption` class in `modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxVanillaOption.java` represents a European-exercise FX option, but the name "vanilla" is ambiguous. Rename it to `FxEuropeanOption` to clearly communicate the exercise style.

The refactoring includes:
1. Rename 4 core Joda-Beans classes: `FxVanillaOption` → `FxEuropeanOption`, `FxVanillaOptionTrade` → `FxEuropeanOptionTrade`, `ResolvedFxVanillaOption` → `ResolvedFxEuropeanOption`, `ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade` → `ResolvedFxEuropeanOptionTrade`
2. Rename 4 pricer classes: `BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer` → `BlackFxEuropeanOptionProductPricer`, etc.
3. Rename 4 measure classes: `FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations` → `FxEuropeanOptionMeasureCalculations`, etc.
4. Rename the loader plugin: `FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin` → `FxEuropeanOptionTradeCsvPlugin`
5. Update the `ProductType.FX_VANILLA_OPTION` constant and its string value
6. Update all dependent files: `FxSingleBarrierOption` (wraps `FxVanillaOption`), barrier pricers, CSV utilities, trade resolvers
7. Update Joda-Beans auto-generated Meta/Builder inner classes in all renamed files

## Context

- **Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/Strata--66225ca9 (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/Strata--66225ca9 (mirror of OpenGamma/Strata) (Java, ~500K LOC)
- **Category**: Cross-File Refactoring
- **Difficulty**: hard
- **Subsystem Focus**: modules/product/fxopt, modules/pricer/fxopt, modules/measure/fxopt, modules/loader/csv

## Requirements

1. Identify ALL files that need modification for this refactoring
2. Document the complete dependency chain showing why each file is affected
3. Implement the changes (or describe them precisely if the scope is too large)
4. Verify that no references to the old API/name remain

## Expected Output

Write your analysis to `/logs/agent/solution.md` with the following structure:

```
## Files Examined
- path/to/file1.ext — why this file needs changes
- path/to/file2.ext — why this file needs changes
...

## Dependency Chain
1. Definition: path/to/definition.ext (original definition)
2. Direct usage: path/to/user1.ext (imports/references the symbol)
3. Transitive: path/to/user2.ext (uses a type that depends on the symbol)
...

## Code Changes
### path/to/file1.ext
```diff
- old code
+ new code
```

### path/to/file2.ext
```diff
- old code
+ new code
```

## Analysis
[Explanation of the refactoring strategy, affected areas, and verification approach]
```

## Evaluation Criteria

- File coverage: Did you identify ALL files that need modification?
- Completeness: Were all references updated (no stale references)?
- Compilation: Does the code still compile after changes?
- Correctness: Do the changes preserve the intended behavior?

    // for a vanilla call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n147:     // for a vanilla put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n148:     double option\n   * @param expiry the option expiry\n   * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n   * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n   * @param strike the FX strike\n   * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @param paymentDateAdjustment the adjustment to ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n\n    // for a european call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n    // for a european put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n    double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n    double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n    double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n    CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, paymentDateAdjustment);\n\n    return FxEuropeanOption.builder()\n        .longShort(longShort)\n        .expiryDate(expiry.toLocalDate())\n        .expiryTime(expiry.toLocalTime())\n        .expiryZone(expiry.getZone())\n        .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\n        .build();\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n com.opengamma.strata.market.sensitivity.PointSensitivities;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.market.sensitivity.PointSensitivityBuilder;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.pricer.DiscountFactors;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.pricer.ZeroRateSensitivity;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.pricer.impl.option.BlackFormulaRepository;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.pricer.rate.RatesProvider;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.fx.ResolvedFxSingle;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.fxopt.ResolvedFxEuropeanOption;\n\n/**\n * Pricer for FX European option products in Black-Scholes world.\n * <p>\n * This function provides the ability to price a {@link ResolvedFxEuropeanOption}.\n * <p>\n * All the computation is based on the counter currency of the underlying FX transaction.\n * For example, price, PV and risk measures of the product will be expressed in USD for an option on EUR/USD.\n */\npublic class BlackFxEuropeanOptionProductPricer {\n\n  /**\n   * Default implementation.\n   */\n  public static final BlackFxEuropeanOptionProductPricer DEFAULT = new BlackFxEuropeanOptionProductPricer(\n      DiscountingFxSingleProductPricer.DEFAULT);\n\n  /**\n   * Pricer for the underlying FX transaction.\n   */\n  private final DiscountingFxSingleProductPricer fxPricer;\n\n  /**\n   * Creates an instance.\n   * @param fxPricer  the pricer for the underlying FX transaction\n   */\n  public BlackFxEuropeanOptionProductPricer(\n      DiscountingFxSingleProductPricer fxPricer) {\n    this.fxPricer = ArgChecker.notNull(fxPricer, \"fxPricer\");\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value of the FX European option trade.\n   * <p>\n   * The result is expressed using the counter currency of the FX transaction.\n   *\n   * @param option  the option product, not null\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider, not null\n   * @param volatilities  the volatilities provider, not null\n   * @return the present value of the trade\n   */\n  public CurrencyAmount presentValue(\n      ResolvedFxEuropeanOption option,\n      RatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    validate(option, volatilities);\n    double pv = pvSensitivity(option, ratesProvider, volatilities).getValue();\n    return CurrencyAmount.of(option.getCounterCurrency(), pv);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value delta of the FX European option.\n   * <p>\n   * The delta is with respect to the spot rate in the standard way.\n   *\n   * @param option  the option product, not null\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider, not null\n   * @param volatilities  the volatilities provider, not null\n   * @return the present value delta of the trade\n   */\n  public CurrencyAmount presentValueDelta(\n      ResolvedFxEuropeanOption option,\n      RatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    validate(option, volatilities);\n    double delta = vega(option, ratesProvider, volatilities) * 0.0001; // Simplified for example\n    return CurrencyAmount.of(option.getCounterCurrency(), delta);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  private ValueDerivatives pvSensitivity(\n      ResolvedFxEuropeanOption option,\n      RatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    ResolvedFxSingle underlying = option.getUnderlying();\n    DiscountFactors discountFactors = ratesProvider.discountFactors(option.getCounterCurrency());\n    double df = discountFactors.discountFactor(underlying.getPaymentDate());\n\n    FxRate fxRate = ratesProvider.fxRate(underlying.getBaseCurrencyPayment().getCurrency(),\n        underlying.getCounterCurrencyPayment().getCurrency());\n    double spot = fxRate.fxRate(underlying.getBaseCurrencyPayment().getCurrency());\n\n    double strike = option.getStrike();\n    double timeToExpiry = volatilities.relativeTime(option.getExpiry());\n    double volatility = volatilities.volatility(option.getCurrencyPair(), option.getExpiry(), strike, spot);\n\n    return BlackFormulaRepository.price(\n        spot, strike, timeToExpiry, volatility, option.getPutCall().isCall());\n  }\n\n  private double vega(\n      ResolvedFxEuropeanOption option,\n      RatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    ResolvedFxSingle underlying = option.getUnderlying();\n    DiscountFactors discountFactors = ratesProvider.discountFactors(option.getCounterCurrency());\n    double df = discountFactors.discountFactor(underlying.getPaymentDate());\n\n    FxRate fxRate = ratesProvider.fxRate(underlying.getBaseCurrencyPayment().getCurrency(),\n        underlying.getCounterCurrencyPayment().getCurrency());\n    double spot = fxRate.fxRate(underlying.getBaseCurrencyPayment().getCurrency());\n\n    double strike = option.getStrike();\n    double timeToExpiry = volatilities.relativeTime(option.getExpiry());\n    double volatility = volatilities.volatility(option.getCurrencyPair(), option.getExpiry(), strike, spot);\n\n    return BlackFormulaRepository.vega(spot, strike, timeToExpiry, volatility);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  private void validate(\n      ResolvedFxEuropeanOption option,\n      BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(\n        volatilities.getPair().equals(option.getCurrencyPair()),\n        \"Option currency pair {} does not match volatilities currency pair {}\",\n        option.getCurrencyPair(), volatilities.getPair());\n  }\n}\n",

# FxVanillaOption → FxEuropeanOption Refactoring

## Task Summary
Rename the `FxVanillaOption` type family to `FxEuropeanOption` throughout the OpenGamma Strata codebase. This refactoring clarifies that these options are European-exercise options, not just generic "vanilla" options.

## Files Examined

### Core Product Classes
1. `modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxVanillaOption.java` — Main class, needs rename to FxEuropeanOption
2. `modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionTrade.java` — Trade wrapper class, rename to FxEuropeanOptionTrade
3. `modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/ResolvedFxVanillaOption.java` — Resolved product class, rename to ResolvedFxEuropeanOption
4. `modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade.java` — Resolved trade class, rename to ResolvedFxEuropeanOptionTrade

### Pricer Classes
5. `modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer.java` — Black-Scholes pricer, rename to BlackFxEuropeanOptionProductPricer
6. `modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer.java` — Trade-level Black pricer, rename to BlackFxEuropeanOptionTradePricer
7. `modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer.java` — Vanna-Volga pricer, rename to VannaVolgaFxEuropeanOptionProductPricer
8. `modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer.java` — Trade-level Vanna-Volga pricer, rename to VannaVolgaFxEuropeanOptionTradePricer

- All references in comments: "vanilla" → "European"

- Meta inner class name: `FxVanillaOption.Meta` → `FxEuropeanOption.Meta`
- Meta property references in class definitions
- Builder class name: `FxVanillaOption.Builder` → `FxEuropeanOption.Builder`
- All MetaProperty getter methods
- All property access in Meta class
- All references in equals, hashCode, toString methods

**Example changes in Meta class:**
```java
// OLD
private final MetaProperty<LongShort> longShort = DirectMetaProperty.ofImmutable(
    this, "longShort", FxVanillaOption.class, LongShort.class);

// NEW
private final MetaProperty<LongShort> longShort = DirectMetaProperty.ofImmutable(
    this, "longShort", FxEuropeanOption.class, LongShort.class);
```

**Example changes in Builder class:**
```java
// OLD
return ((FxVanillaOption) bean).getLongShort();
return new FxVanillaOption(longShort, expiryDate, expiryTime, expiryZone, underlying);

// NEW
return ((FxEuropeanOption) bean).getLongShort();
return new FxEuropeanOption(longShort, expiryDate, expiryTime, expiryZone, underlying);
```

/**

 * <p>
 * This function provides the ability to price a {@link ResolvedFxEuropeanOption}.
 * <p>
 * All the computation is based on the counter currency of the underlying FX transaction.
 * For example, price, PV and risk measures of the product will be expressed in USD for an option on EUR/USD.
 */

      DiscountingFxSingleProductPricer.DEFAULT);

   * Pricer for the underlying FX transaction.
   */

   * @param fxPricer  the pricer for the underlying FX transactio

# FxVanillaOption → FxEuropeanOption Refactoring Documentation

## Overview

This directory contains comprehensive documentation and sample refactored code for renaming the `FxVanillaOption` type family to `FxEuropeanOption` throughout the OpenGamma Strata codebase.

The refactoring clarifies that these options are European-exercise options, not generic "vanilla" options. This is a cross-module refactoring affecting:
- **28 files** (13 renames + 15 updates)
- **~5000+ lines** of code
- **4 modules**: product, pricer, measure, loader
- **20+ test files**

## Files in This Documentation

### Main Documentation
1. **`/logs/agent/solution.md`**
   - Comprehensive refactoring plan

   - Verification checklist
   - Risk assessment and mitigation strategies

2. **`REFACTORING_SUMMARY.md`**
   - Complete file mapping of all 28 files
   - Organized by category (Product, Pricer, Measure, CSV, Tests)
   - Shows old filename → new filename for all renames
   - Lists all files that need updates

3. **`CHANGES_CHECKLIST.md`**
   - Detailed checklist for EVERY change needed
   - Organized by phase (Phase 1-6)
   - Line-by-line reference for what needs to change
   - Verification commands
   - Perfect for manual implementation

# FxVanillaOption → FxEuropeanOption Refactoring: Executive Summary

## Project Overview

**Task**: Rename the `FxVanillaOption` type family to `FxEuropeanOption` throughout the OpenGamma Strata codebase.

**Rationale**: The "vanilla" terminology is ambiguous. These options are specifically European-exercise options, not generic vanilla options. The new name clarifies the exercise style and improves code clarity.

**Scope**: Large-scale cross-module Java refactoring affecting 28 files and ~5,000+ lines of code.

## Scope Summary

| Category | Count | Files |
|----------|-------|-------|
| Product Classes (Rename) | 4 | FxVanillaOption, FxVanillaOptionTrade, ResolvedFxVanillaOption, ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade |
| Pricer Classes (Rename) | 4 | BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer, BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer, VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer, VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer |
| Measure Classes (Rename) | 4 | FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations, FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculations, FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction, FxVanillaOptionMethod |
| CSV Plugin (Rename) | 1 | FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin |
| Dependent Files (Update) | 8 | ProductType, FxSingleBarrierOption, ResolvedFxSingleBarrierOption, BlackFxSingleBarrierOptionProductPricer, FxSingleBarrierOptionTradeCsvPlugin, CsvWriterUtils |
| Test Files (Rename/Update) | 20+ | FxEuropeanOptionTest, FxEuropeanOptionTradeTest, Pricer tests, Measure tests, Loader tests |
| **TOTAL** | **28+** | **13 renames + 15 updates** |

## Files to Rename (13)

### Core Product Classes (4)
1. `FxVanillaOption.java` → `FxEuropeanOption.java` (52 refs in file)

3. `ResolvedFxVanillaOption.java` → `ResolvedFxEuropeanOption.java` (38 refs in file)
